<Date>1547269233974<//Date><Rating>3< /Rating><text>The food here is great, but the service we received was terrible. We ordered the Garlic edamame, Touchdown Roll (tempura shrimp, assorted seafood, eel sauce, tempura bits), and Happy Roll (spicy tuna, shrimp tempura, avocado, eel). All of these were delicious! But sadly that's about all the good there was. Terrible service seemed to be the theme of the night. We of the 3 groups of 2 that we're waiting, the wait staff pulled the newest group to be seated. When the hostess was notified she looked frustrated and apologized for that, but didn't do much else for the remaining 2 groups left. When we were seated it took a bit before we were able to even place a drink let alone food order. While waiting it was evident that all the tables around us had orders that were forgotten or missed.  The table that seemed to have been there the longest had at least 3 things they ordered but never came.

Despite the service, I will give this place another shot on a different day, if only for that garlic edamame.</text>< Pictures>

I truly hate going to the dentist.  I always feel the pain of any procedure even after getting novocain.  Let me begin with Elaine. She is a very sweet lady.
